var UserStatus = "anonymous";

function createCookie(name,value,days) { if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}
function eraseCookie(name) {
createCookie(name,"",-1);
}
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
return null;
}
function deleteCookie(name) {
createCookiewithdomain(name,null,-1);
}
function createCookiewithdomain(name,value,days) {
if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; domain="+document.location.host.match(/\.[.\w]*/)+";path=/";
}
function getStorage(name){	if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {	if (localStorage.getItem(name)){	cookieObj = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(name));
if (cookieObj !== undefined && (cookieObj.e == null || cookieObj.e > new Date())){return cookieObj.v === undefined ? null : cookieObj.v ; }	else{localStorage.removeItem(name);}	}
return null;	} else {return readCookie(name);}	}
function setStorage(name,value,days){
if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {
var date = new Date();	localStorage.setItem(name,JSON.stringify({"v":value, "e":date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000))}))
} else {createCookie(name,value,days);}	}
function eraseStorage(name){ if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {localStorage.removeItem(name);}
else{eraseCookie(name)}
}
function getUrlParameter( name, url ) {
if (!url) url = location.href;
name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
var regex = new RegExp(regexS,"i");
var results = regex.exec( url );
return results == null ? null : results[1];
}
function getHostName(){
return window.location.hostname;
} function loadAsyncURL(url){ var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
s.type = "text/javascript";
s.async = true; s.src = url; el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
}
function loadSyncURL(url){ var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
s.type = "text/javascript";
s.src = url; el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
}
function loadPromiseScript(src) {
return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
let script = document.createElement('script');
script.src = src;
script.async = true;
script.onload = function(){
resolve(script);
}
document.head.append(script);
});
}
function crossfetchGet(url,fn){
// Default options are marked with *
return fetch(url, {
method: 'GET', // *GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, etc.
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include', // include, *same-origin, omit
}).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.reject();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.reject();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}	function crossfetchPost(url, data, fn) {
return fetch(url, {
method: 'POST',
body: JSON.stringify(data),
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include', // include, *same-origin, omit
}).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}
function fetchtimeout(ms,url,options,fn) {
const FETCH_TIMEOUT = ms;
let didTimeOut = false;
return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
const timeout = setTimeout(function() {
didTimeOut = true;
reject(new Error('Request timed out -> ' +ms +" ms"));
}, FETCH_TIMEOUT);
fetch(url,options).then(function(response) {
// Clear the timeout as cleanup
clearTimeout(timeout);
if(!didTimeOut) {
resolve(response);
}
})
.catch(function(err) {
// Rejection already happened with setTimeout
if(didTimeOut) return;
// Reject with error
reject(err);
//	console.error(err.message +"= "+url);
})
}).then(function(response) {
// Request success and no timeout
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else
{
console.error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText); }
})
.then(function(response) {
fn(response);
})
.catch(function(err) {
// Error: response error, request timeout or runtime error
console.error(err.message +"= "+url);
return Promise.resolve();
//return Promise.reject();
})
}
function fetchApi(url,options,fn) {
return fetch(url,options).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}

function guidId() {
if(readCookie("browserDeviceId") != null){
return readCookie("browserDeviceId");
}
else{
var nav = window.navigator;
var screen = window.screen;
// var guid = nav.mimeTypes.length;
var guid = nav.userAgent.replace(/\D+/g, '');
// guid += nav.plugins.length;
guid += screen.height || '';
guid += screen.width || '';
guid += screen.pixelDepth || '';
createCookiewithdomain("browserDeviceId",guid,365);
return guid;
}
};
var subscription = {siteId: "TRC-J3AFTO",deviceId: guidId()};const siteId = function(){return subscription.siteId;};const deviceId = function (){return subscription.deviceId;};
var userId = "";
if (!String.prototype.includes) {
String.prototype.includes = function(search, start) {
if (typeof start !== 'number') {
start = 0;
}
if (start + search.length > this.length) {
return false;
} else {
return this.indexOf(search, start) !== -1;
}
};
}

<script>
userIdentify.then(function() {
if (userId != "") {
isloggedinUser();
if(isNonSubcribedUser() && !migratedUser){
document.getElementsByClassName("mobileadsubentry")[0].style.display = "block";
typeof document.getElementsByClassName("mobileadsubentryfreetrail")[0] !="undefined" ? document.getElementsByClassName("mobileadsubentryfreetrail")[0].remove() : null;
document.getElementsByClassName("mobileadsubentryremoveads")[0].innerText ="Subscribe Now"
}
}
else{
document.getElementsByClassName("mobileadsubentry")[0].style.display = "block";
}
});
function daysleft(enddate){
var day_start = new Date();
var day_end = new Date(enddate);
day_end.setHours(23,59,59,999);
var enddatefinal = new Date(day_end);
var total_days = (enddatefinal - day_start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
total_days = total_days - 1;
if(Math.ceil(total_days) < 1){
total_days = "0";
}
return Math.ceil(total_days);
}
function logout(){
if(typeof sendTaiData !== "undefined") {
taiDataObject['etime'] = "" + new Date().getTime();
taiDataObject['userinfo'] = isUserDetails;
taiData.push(taiDataObject);
sendTaiData(taiData, 'signout');
}
fetchApi("https://tai.thehindu.com/v1/auth/logout/HINDU",{
method: 'POST',
body: JSON.stringify({"userId":userId,"deviceId":deviceId(), "siteId":"TRC-J3AFTO"}),
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include' // include, *same-origin, omit
},function(res){
if(res.status == "success"){
deleteCookie("thuser");
window.location.reload();
}
else if (typeof res.reason != "undefined" && res.reason == 1){
deleteCookie("thuser");
window.location.reload();
}
}); }
function isloggedinUser() {
var userFullName = JSON.parse(isUserDetails.userInfo);
var userName = userFullName.FullName;
if (userName != "") {
userName = "Hi " + userName;
} else if (isUserDetails.userName != ""
&& isUserDetails.userName != undefined) {
userName = "Hi " + isUserDetails.userName;
} else {
userName = "Hi user";
}
document.getElementById("sso-signin").innerText = userName;
var dropdown = '<ul class="dropdown-menu sso-signinuser">'
+ '<li class="mobileusername" ><a class="" >'
+ userName
+ '</a>'
+ '<li class="Subscribebtnremove" data-category="Hi user" data-label="SUBSCRIBE NOW"><a class="Subscribebtn" href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/subscription?utm_source=thusermenu&utm_medium=subscribebutton&utm_campaign=subscription">Subscribe Now</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My Dashboard"><a href="/my-dashboard/" class="sso-profile">My Dashboard</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My profile"><a href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/profile" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">My Profile</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Personalization"><a href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/profile?info=preference" class="sso-profile infopersonal">Personalisation</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My Plan"><a href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/profile?info=subscriptioninfo" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">My Plan</a>'
+'<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Transaction History"><a href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/profile?info=transactioninfo" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">Transaction History</a>'
+'<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Feedback"><a href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/profile?info=feedback" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">Feedback</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="FAQ"><a href="https://subscription.thehindu.com/faq" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">FAQS</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Contact us"><a href="https://www.thehindu.com/contacts/" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">Contact Us</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Sign Out"><a class="sso-logout" onclick="logout()" >Sign Out</a>'
+ '</ul>';
document.getElementById("sso-signin").removeAttribute("href");
document.getElementById("sso-signin").classList.remove("sso-signin");
document.getElementById("mobilesigninlink").removeAttribute("href")
document.getElementById("mobilesignin").classList.remove("sso-signin");
document.getElementById("mobilesignin").classList
.add("sso-signinmobile");
var els = document
.querySelectorAll("#main-menu>ul>li:nth-last-child(-n+2)");
[].forEach.call(els, function(els) {
els.style.display = "none";
});
document.getElementsByClassName("subsEntrymenu")[0].style.display = "block";
document.getElementsByClassName("submobileentry")[0].style.display = "block";
var list = document.querySelectorAll(".signinbtn");
for (var i = 0; i < list.length; ++i) {
list[i].classList.add('ssologin');
list[i].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', dropdown);
}
var listmobile = document.querySelectorAll(".sigininmobile");
for (var i = 0; i < listmobile.length; ++i) {
listmobile[i].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', dropdown);
}
var NextRenewalDate = isUserDetails.nextRenewalDate;
if(typeof isUserDetails.nextRenewalDate == "undefined"){
NextRenewalDate = 0;
}
if (isUserDetails.userPlanList.length > 0) {
for (var j = 0; j < isUserDetails.userPlanList.length; ++j) {
if (isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].status == "success" && isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].amount != "0" && daysleft(NextRenewalDate) > 10 ) {
var btnremove = document.querySelectorAll(".Subscribebtnremove");
SubscribedUserPlan.purchased = true;
for (var m = 0; m < btnremove.length; ++m) {
btnremove[m].style.display = "none";
}
}
else if(isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].status == "success" && isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].amount == "0" && daysleft(NextRenewalDate) > 30){
var btnremove = document.querySelectorAll(".Subscribebtnremove");
SubscribedUserPlan.purchased = true;
for (var m = 0; m < btnremove.length; ++m) {
btnremove[m].style.display = "none";
}
}
else if (isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].status == "success" && isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].amount != "0") {
SubscribedUserPlan.purchased = true;
}
else if (isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].status == "success" && isUserDetails.userPlanList[j].amount == "0") {
SubscribedUserPlan.freetrail = true;
}
}
}
}

hidedd = true;
});
});

<div class=" ">
<h2 class="intro">
Close to 90% of those surveyed did not get paid by their employers
</h2>
<div id="content-body-14269002-31384413">
<p>A survey of 11,159 <a href="https://www.thehindu.com/news/national/telangana/not-all-migrant-workers-received-dry-rations/article31376959.ece">migrant workers</a> stranded in various States found that between April 8 and April 13, more than 90% did not receive <a href="https://www.thehindu.com/opinion/lead/shift-to-upscaling-food-rationing-now/article31186819.ece">rations </a>from the government. Close to 90% of those surveyed did not get paid by their employers. From March 27 to April 13, 70% of the surveyed workers had only less than ₹200 left with them. </p><p>The survey was conducted by the Stranded Workers Action Network (SWAN). <strong><a href="https://www.thehindu.com/news/resources/article31442220.ece/binary/Lockdown-and-Distress_Report-by-Stranded-Workers-Action-Network.pdf">Click here</a></strong> to read the full report.</p><h2>Low on food and money</h2><p>The chart shows the % of migrant workers who did not receive rations or cooked food from the government/ other sources, and were not paid by employers, between April 8 and April 13. While in this period, the % of workers who received cooked food from the government/ other sources improved marginally, most of them did not receive rations from the government or wages from their employers.</p><p><strong>Did the stranded workers receive essentials?</strong></p><p>
<div class="data
article-block-item ">

 </p><p>As a high share of migrants workers received neither rations nor cooked food from the government/NGOs, and were not paid their salaries, the share of workers having less than one day of rations left increased steadily.</p><p><strong>Also read:  <a href="https://www.thehindu.com/data/covid-19-state-wise-tracker-for-coronavirus-cases-deaths-and-testing-rates/article31248444.ece?homepage=true#comments_31248444">COVID-19 | State-wise tracker for coronavirus cases, deaths and testing rates</a></strong></p><h2>Worst hit States</h2><p>The following points list the % of migrant workers left without essential items such as rations and cooked food, and the % of those who had less than ₹200 to survive, between March 27 and April 13. Workers stranded in Uttar Pradesh were among the worst affected.</p><h3>Left without rations</h3><p><strong>96% workers surveyed across India said they did not get rations from the government.</strong></p><ul><li>In Uttar Pradesh, 100% of the migrant workers did not receive rations</li><li>In Maharashtra, 99% of them did not receive rations.</li><li>In Karnataka, 93% of them did not receive rations.</li></ul><h3>Without cooked food</h3><p><strong>70% workers surveyed across India said they did not get cooked food from the government or local organisations.</strong></p><ul><li>In Uttar Pradesh, 64% migrant workers did not receive cooked food.</li><li>In Karnataka, 80% did not receive cooked food; in Maharashtra, it was 58%; and in Delhi and Haryana it was 66%.</li></ul><h3>State of existing rations</h3><p><strong>70% workers surveyed across India said existing rations would last them only for two days.</strong></p><ul><li>In Uttar Pradesh, 100% of the migrant workers said that rations would last them only for 2 days.</li><li>In Maharashtra, 90% said the same.</li><li>In Delhi and Haryana, 82% said the same.</li></ul><h3>State of finances</h3><p><strong>70% workers surveyed across India said they had less than ₹200 to survive during the lockdown.</strong></p><ul><li>In Uttar Pradesh, 87% of the migrant workers had less than ₹200.</li><li>In Haryana, 76% had less than ₹300</li></ul><p><strong>Also read: <a href="https://www.thehindu.com/news/national/coronavirus-confusion-in-india-over-mismatch-in-numbers-of-health-ministry-apex-medical-body-icmr/article31384074.ece?homepage=true">Coronavirus | Confusion over mismatch in Health Ministry, ICMR figures</a></strong></p>
</div>

if (offset > 1) {

}
if (max > -1) {
$("#content-body-14269002-31384413").children().slice(max).remove();
}
// Show dateline field at the beginning of the first paragraph
var showDateline = false;
var datelineStr = "";
if (offset <= 1 && showDateline == true && datelineStr != "") {
var firstChild = $("#content-body-14269002-31384413").children().get(0);
if ("P" == firstChild.nodeName.toUpperCase()) {
$(firstChild).prepend("<span>" + datelineStr + " - </span>");
}
else {
$(firstChild).before("<span>" + datelineStr + "</span>");
}
}
});
</script>
<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
$('a.tweetable').click(function(){
var text = $(this).text();
$('[href*="#"]').attr('href', 'https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text='+text+" "+url);
});
});
</script>

.nopad{padding:0px;}
</style>

<script>
var comFetch;
var emailAddressFilter = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/;
function validate_email(fieldId) {
var email = $(fieldId).val();
email= email.trim();
if (email == "" || email == "undefined") {
return false;
} else if (!emailAddressFilter.test(email)) {
return false;
}
return true;
}
//<!-- article page contains multiple times if infinite scroll is enabled. -->
$(document).ready(function(){

$(this).attr("disabled","disabled");
var selector = $(this).closest(".LeftLetterSrch");
$(selector).find("input").click(function(){$(selector).find("button").removeAttr("disabled");});
var email = $(selector).find("input").val();
email= email.trim();
$(selector).find(".nl-error").css("display", "none");
$(selector).find(".nl-success").css("display", "none");
$(selector).find("input").removeClass("error");
if (validate_email($(selector).find("input"))){ if(typeof sendTaiData !== "undefined" ) {
taiData.push({"email":email});
sendTaiData(taiData, 'newslettersub');
}
$(selector).find(".nl-load").show();
$(selector).find(".nl-load").addClass("active");
var url = publist("url") + "s/mailsubscription/subscribe/";
var data = {"email" : email, "category" : "dt"};
var s = fetchPost(url,data);
s.then(function(result) {
document.getElementById("demo").innerHTML=result.data;
});
} else { $(selector).find(".nl-load").fadeOut( "slow");
$(selector).find(".nl-error").css("display", "block");
$(selector).find("input").addClass("error");
}
});
});
</script>

if(typeof secondPTag !== "undefined"){
Element.prototype.appendAfter = function(element) {
element.parentNode.insertBefore(this, element.nextSibling);
};
var newElement = document.createElement('div');
newElement.id = slotName;
newElement.setAttribute("class", "dfp-ad");
newElement.appendAfter(secondPTag);
break;
}
}
}
}
googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1518418788389-1'); });
}
});
</script>

</div>
</div>

<script>
$(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).on("makeSocialShareReady", function(event, data) {
var selector = $(data).find(".hover-social-media-top ul li, .hover-social-media-bottom ul li");
$(selector).on('click', function (e) {
var shareUrl = $(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('share-url');
var shareText = $(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('share-text');
var shareValue ="";
if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-facebook')) {
shareValue = "facebook";
openShareLink('http://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
} else if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-twitter')) {
shareValue = "twitter";
openShareLink('http://twitter.com/share?text=' + encodeURIComponent(shareText) + '&url=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
}
if(typeof sendTaiData !== "undefined" && shareValue != "") {
taiDataObject['share'] = shareValue;
taiDataObject['etime'] = "" + new Date().getTime();
taiData.push(taiDataObject);
sendTaiData(taiData, 'share');
}
});
});
$(document).on('pageContentReady', function (event, content) {
$(document).trigger( "makeSocialShareReady", content );
});
});
$(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).trigger( "makeSocialShareReady", $('body') );
});
function openShareLink(pLink) {
var popUp = window.open(pLink, 'popupwindow', 'scrollbars=yes,width=740,height=400');
popUp.focus();
return false;
}
</script>

$(document).ready(function(e){

var selector = $(data).find("ul.aricle-share:last li a");
$(selector).on('click',function(e){
if($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-print')) {
window.print();
} else {	if(typeof $(this).find("i").attr("class") !="undefined") {
var targetClass = $(this).find("i").attr("class").split(" ")[1];
if(excludeShareClickList.indexOf(targetClass) === -1 ) {
if(typeof sendTaiData !== "undefined" ) {
taiDataObject['share'] = targetClass.split("-")[1];

sendTaiData(taiData, 'share');
}
var id = $(".jscroll-inner>.active .articlepage").data("artid") + "-" + targetClass;
openShareLink(articleShareData[id]);
}
}
}
});
});

}
});

return false;
}

"K": 1000
};
_renderShareCount = function(share, container) {
var $count = $(container).next('.cnt');
this._loadCount(share).done($.proxy(function(count) {
if(count) {
$count.text(count);
}
}, this));
}
_loadCount = function(share) {
var deferred = $.Deferred();
var countUrl = this._getCountUrl(share);
if(!countUrl) {
return deferred.resolve(0).promise();
}
var handleSuccess = $.proxy(function(response) {
deferred.resolve(this._getCountValue(response, share));
}, this);
$.getJSON(countUrl).done(handleSuccess)
.fail(function() {
$.get(countUrl).done(handleSuccess)
.fail(function() {
deferred.resolve(0);
});
});
return deferred.promise();
}
_getShareUrl = function(share) {
var shareUrl = getOrApply(share.shareUrl, share);
return this._formatShareUrl(shareUrl, share);
}
_getCountUrl = function(share) {
var countUrl = getOrApply(share.countUrl, share);
return this._formatShareUrl(countUrl, share);
}
_getCountValue = function(response, share) {
var count = ($.isFunction(share.getCount) ? share.getCount(response) : response) || 0;
return (typeof count === "string") ? count : this._formatNumber(count);
}
_formatNumber = function(number) {
$.each(MEASURES, function(letter, value) {
if(number >= value) {
number = parseFloat((number / value).toFixed(2)) + letter;
return false;
}
});
return number;
}
_formatShareUrl = function(url, share) {
return url.replace(URL_PARAMS_REGEX, function(match, key, field) {
var value = share[field] || "";
return value ? (key || "") + window.encodeURIComponent(value) : "";
});
}
_createSelector = function(identifier) {
var tmp = "";
for(var i=0; i<selectorArray.length; i++) {
tmp += "."+selectorArray[i]+" ."+identifier;
if(selectorArray.length > 1 && i < (selectorArray.length - 1))
tmp += ", ";
}
return tmp;
}
var tmpCards = new Array();
var tmpArray = ["facebook", "twitter", "reddit", "whatsapp", "webwhatsapp", "email"];
for(i = 0; i < tmpArray.length; i++) { tmpCards.push(socialCards[tmpArray[i]]);
}
$.each(tmpCards, function(index){
var share = tmpCards[index];
share.url = url;
share.text = text;
_renderShareCount(share, _createSelector(share.faClass));
sUrl = _getShareUrl(share);
// share.shareUrl = sUrl;
var tmpKey = articleId + "-" + share.faClass;	articleShareData[tmpKey] = sUrl;
});
var shareWhatsapp = socialCards.whatsapp;
var shareUrlswhatsapp = articleShareData[articleId + "-" + shareWhatsapp.faClass];
shareUrlswhatsapp += window.encodeURIComponent("?utm_campaign=article_share&utm_medium=referral&utm_source=whatsapp.com");
var myWhatsappFunction = function() {
window.open(shareUrlswhatsapp, "_blank", "toolbar=yes,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,top=0,left=0,width=800,height=400");
}
$(data).find('.fa-whatsapp.wa').parent().on('click',myWhatsappFunction);	$(".sticky-article-heading ul.aricle-sticky-share li i.fa-whatsapp.wa").parent().on('click',myWhatsappFunction);
var shareenvelope = socialCards.email;
shareEnvelopeUrl = articleShareData[articleId + "-" + shareenvelope.faClass];
$(data).find('.fa-envelope.en').parent().attr("href", shareEnvelopeUrl)
.attr("target", "_" + shareenvelope.shareIn);
$(".sticky-article-heading ul.aricle-sticky-share li i.fa-envelope.en").parent().attr("href", shareEnvelopeUrl)
.attr("target", "_" + shareenvelope.shareIn);
});	});
$(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).trigger( "articleSocialShareReady", $('.articlepage:last'));
});
var socialCards = {
facebook: {
faClass : 'fa-facebook',
shareUrl: "https://facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u={url}",
countUrl: function() {
return "https://graph.facebook.com/?id={url}";
},
getCount: function(data) {
return (data.share && data.share.share_count) || 0;
}
},
googleplus: {
faClass : 'fa-google-plus',
shareUrl: "https://plus.google.com/share?url={url}",
countUrl: function() {
return "https://cors-anywhere.herokuapp.com/https://plusone.google.com/_/+1/fastbutton?url="+ window.encodeURIComponent(this.url);
},
getCount: function(data) {
return parseFloat((data.match(/\{c: ([.0-9E]+)/) || [])[1]);
}
},
linkedin: {
faClass : 'fa-linkedin',
shareUrl: "https://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url={url}",
countUrl: "https://www.linkedin.com/countserv/count/share?format=jsonp&url={url}&callback=?",
getCount: function(data) {
return data.count;
}
},
pinterest: {
faClass : 'fa-pinterest-p',
shareUrl: "https://pinterest.com/pin/create/bookmarklet/?media={media}&url={url}&description={text}",
countUrl: "https://api.pinterest.com/v1/urls/count.json?&url={url}&callback=?",
getCount: function(data) {
return data.count;
}
},
stumbleupon: {
faClass : 'fa-stumbleupon',
shareUrl: "http://www.stumbleupon.com/submit?url={url}&title={title}",
countUrl: "https://cors-anywhere.herokuapp.com/https://www.stumbleupon.com/services/1.01/badge.getinfo?url={url}",
getCount: function(data) {
return data.result.views;
}
},
twitter: {
faClass : 'fa-twitter',
shareUrl: "https://twitter.com/share?url={url}&text={text}&via={via}&hashtags={hashtags}",
countUrl: ""
},
whatsapp: {
faClass: "fa-whatsapp",
shareUrl: "whatsapp://send?text={text} {url}",
countUrl: "",
shareIn: "blank"
},
webwhatsapp: {
faClass: "fa-whatsapp",
shareUrl: "https://api.whatsapp.com/send?text={text} {url}",
countUrl: "",
shareIn: "blank"
},
email: {
faClass : 'fa-envelope',
shareUrl: "mailto:{to}?subject={text}&body={url}",
countUrl: "",
shareIn: "self"
},
gmail: {
faClass : 'fa-envelope',
shareUrl: "https://mail.google.com/mail/u/0/?view=cm&fs=1&to=&su={text}&body={url}",
countUrl: "",
shareIn: "blank"
},
reddit: {
faClass : 'fa-reddit-alien',
shareUrl: "https://reddit.com/submit?url={url}&title={title}",
countUrl: "https://www.reddit.com/api/info.json?url=",
getCount: function(response) {
var childrens = response.data.children;
if(childrens.length > 0) {
if(childrens[0].hasOwnProperty("data")) {
return childrens[0].data.score;
}
}
return "";
}
}
}
